<Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
This review is specifically about the Small Group Training (SGT) at the Culver City Anytime Fitness location.  First off, the SGT is expensive.  BUT...it is completely worth it!  Usually there are only two or three other individuals participating in a given group and it feels as if you have a personal trainer.  I have been participating in SGT for several months with Cruz and he is fantastic!  Cruz will structure the one-hour workout to your ability level and continue to push you past what you think are your limits.  He has increased my knowledge about pre-workout warm ups and full body exercise routines (with and without weights).  I have been very active in fitness for two decades and am happy to have Cruz push me hard in every workout.  Over the past several months these workouts have added a jolt to my fitness level and motivation.

My recommendation is to sign up for a set package of 2 SGTs per week and then apply what you learn to your other workouts during the week.  This is especially relevant to the exercises you learn for abs.

A note about the facility: they recently remodeled this gym and it is very nice!  It doesn't have a dedicated setup for power lifting, but the power racks are usually available if you want to do dead lifts or power cleans.<//text>

<Text>Have loved this place for over a decade, and still consider it one of my fave secret spots for impressing die-hard sushi lovers. <user_id>114726736107421909335<//user_id>< resp>

<date>1541110653161</date><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
I cannot recommend Zushi Puzzle enough! Their Omakase experience is amazing. I'll start by saying make sure if you would like to try the Omakase that you have a reservation. It's typically very full, so call ahead to make sure you have a spot. Chef Roger and his team of sous chefs are so much fun! Making the experience that much better! They really listen to their customers to customize the experience they are having. In fact another couple was having a birthday there and they picked up on that without being explicitly told. It's the small things that count.

Regarding the food, AMAZING! The small truffle additions to some of the nigiri was perfect. I've never had truffle on sushi before but I highly recommend trying it. The uni was very unique as well, I believe chef Roger is known for a special sushi dish with uni on it. The fish was amazing and he talked about sourcing fish and the different kinds throughout our meal, even educating us on how to eat sushi (make sure the fish is down so you get that flavor first). We had a special request for Kobe beef as well and of course he delivered! It was amazing!

Dessert was the most unique ever as well. He had a Kobe beef ice cream and similar savory but sweet ice creams. It sounds a bit unnerving but it was so smooth, creamy and flavorful (enough for the few bites given for dessert).

The price tag is a bit high, but not too high for a special occasion or fun night out. I highly recommend Zushi Puzzle and I will certainly be back if I'm in San Francisco again.<//Text>

<Review>Decided to 'pop' in here after a recommendation from a friend of a friend. Sitting at the bar is the way to go. Not that the service at our table wasn't great, but the master chef making us whatever sushi he felt like was an experience.

<user>108230289207003255200<//user><Name>Chris Shellenbarger</Name>< time>
1472274909123</time>
<Rating>5</Rating>< text>
This is our favorite sushi restaurant in SF.  They fly their fish in from all over the world, especially Japan.  Depending on the season, they have 5-8 different types of salmon. Rolls are great as well.

You'll most likely need a reservation unless you come right when they open, but even then I've seen them turn people away.

You can also special order fish from Japan in advance.  A table near us did this and spent over 4k on their complete meal for 4. That's how high end of fish this place can serve if you request it in advance.

For us normal people with a normal budget, zushi puzzle is a reasonably priced with most Nigiri between 5 and 13 dollars.  Rolls are priced from 6-20 depending on size.

The chef Roger is awesome and is rated one of America's Best Chefs.  If you sit at the bar and do omikaze,  he'll ask you what you like and don't like and will make sure you enjoy everything he makes you. He's got a great wit as well!</text>

<text>The omakase is a must. Chef Roger only does 2 seatings a night (6:30 and 8:30) at the bar/chef's table in the back of the restaurant. You will need a reservation, but it's usually not too hard for a weekday. Chef Roger has the freshest fish, and his talents made our anniversary meal amazing! We went through at least 16 courses, but our main sashimi plate was INCREDIBLE. Even the presentation was beautiful!

Chef Rogar is really friendly, but if you would prefer only a few fancy rolls to the omakase experience, the bar may not be the best place. It took us 2 hours to enjoy the full experience, and although it was pricey, well worth the money! We'll definitely be coming more often!</text>< pictures>

<Resp>None< /Resp>< Review>
Oh my god. OH MY GOD!!! One of my favorite meals in SF and maybe in life. Must get omakase at the bar with Roger. He loves and respects food like nobody's business. If you want to eat boring rolls don't come here. If you want a sushi culinary journey then come sit at the bar.

Highlights:
Best handroll
Four kinds of toro
Kobe beef sushi with foie gras
Sweet shrimp and ankimo shavings
His epic ice cream made with KOBE BEEF FAT (its actually delicious)
Fresh scallop sushi
Uni and tofu
Pretty much...everything. Just trust in Roger.

Note: omakase is gonna cost a pretty penny, but better than most 1-2 Michelin seafood places for sure!<//Review>

< Review>
We made reservations and were seated right away by courteous staff and were given complementary edamame which was a nice touch. We ordered salads, two different sushi rolls and a 10 piece of the Chef's choice sashimi. The sushi rolls were good but average. They tasted fresh and tasty but were not anything exceptional at all and we've definitely had better. The sashimi, however, was out of this world. We have never had sashimi so fresh and delicious. If we lived in the area all the time, we'd frequent Zushi puzzle all the time just for their sashimi. Overall, we had a good experience at a very fair price.<//Review>

< review>
Great customer service at this Chevron gas station and convenience store in Fontana, CA. They even have diesel fuel and an air and water station. The gas pumps are clean and the squeegee stations are full of water and there are towels at every station.

<rating>5</rating><text>It is great to go into a market where everyone knows you name. That was what life was like before the tradeoff of price for service left us searching isles for help. For my money and they do get my money, Harvest Ranch Market is a shop where you feel good walking in. It is a friendly experience and you can find almost anything you are looking for. Get to know the manager John Barbat and the staff in the deli and meat/fish counter and you will get their picks for the day (although the meatballs and enchiladas are always worth the trip).
During Covid-19 every extra service has been happily offered including shopping and delivery to the trunk of your car when you pull up. It all adds to the value of being a loyal customer and enjoying the environment of the Mom and Pops that once lined America's main streets. So, with thanks to John for keeping me safe (and always finding enough TP). I recommend that you enjoy your experience at Harvest Ranch and keep a local treasure prosperous.<//text>< pics>

< Text>
We spent hours looking for somewhere to get covid tests to meet travel requirements for the UK. Not only was there no support from our airline or Kaiser, but there was confusing and non-specific information from the British government about which tests and at what sensitivity.

Google searches turned up places that quoted $200, $300 and even $400 - per one-hour PCR test - which for the four of US, with three lots of UK testing once we arrived was approaching the cost of the flights themselves. A CVS appointment, for which I took the morning off work and drove for half an hour each way with two small children, turned me away because I‚Äôd booked ‚Äúthe wrong kind of appointment‚Äù with completely unsympathetic staff.

Luckily a friend mentioned City Health, who had next-day appointments for travel-approved test at no cost, and right in the city rather than down at SFO. Staff were extremely efficient, had lots of safety precautions and were very helpful. The only thing that would‚Äôve made it better would be if they were findable on Google!

Test before noon and you get the results by 2pm next day. Superb service for the city, thank you.<//Text>

<Text>Complaint!!!My disappointment is I was not able to pick up my prescription at Walgreen's. This was because whoever sent prescription did not pay attention to detail. Sharon said my prescription would be ready in 30 minutes. Walgreen's had my birth date wrong. My birthday is in October not February. I presented my identification two times at your office. I was quite disappointed because I really needed to start medication to treat what I came to Urgent Care for. Kind of takes away from the concept if I can't get what I need. I am still in pain and discomfort. I was not able to sleep at all last night. My face is still swollen and skin was inflamed. I called around 3:30 to explain my birth date was incorrect. I requested  for someone to call Walgreen's. Around 5:30, a man called to confirm my birth date. He did not like me asking why did this happen? He seemed not to care very much about my concerns. He told me Walgreen's will send me a text. Did not hear from Walgreen's. Called the pharmacy at 8:30 and they did not have my subscription ready. It is 6:30 in the morning now. I request the prescription to be sent this morning to Walgreen's first thing this morning. I need to start treatment immediately. Don't know if anyone will read this that cares, so I will call as soon as office is open to request this verbally. This was my first visit to Urgent Care and this experience was so horrible I will not use your services again. Whomever submitted incorrect information to Walgreen's needs to be reprimanded. I also would appreciate an apology as well. The man who called me at 5:30 had the opportunity, but instead was making excuses after I inquired "how did this happen".
